2471239					CONF							20000	0	0	0	true		0	0												0	0	0	0														Capital infusion from the Bank Holding Company				Mngt. identified two errors in the prior years? financial statements (?FS?) that were corrected in the 9/30/21 YTD Report of Income. The first item was that accrued interest in prior years was understated due to the improper accounting for a nonaccrual loan. The second item related to the valuation of the mortgage servicing right assets due to use of an inaccurate estimate for the lives of the underlying loans. The prior year cumulative impact of both items on net income as of 12/31/20 was $5.4M. These amounts were corrected as of 9/30/21 and had the impact of increasing loan interest income by $5.1M and other income by $1.1M. Mngt. concluded these amounts to be immaterial to the FS for the years 2018-2020 and for YTD 9/30/21.
